                    //设置舌签的开闭
                    for (var i = 1; i <= 5; i++)
                    {
                        document.getElementById("hq"+i).className = "";
                        document.getElementById("hq"+i+"_Layer").style.display = "none";				
                    }
                    document.getElementById("hq"+id).className = "current";
                    document.getElementById("hq"+id+"_Layer").style.display = "block";
                    
                    if (sign_map[id] == 'false') {
                        document.getElementById("hq"+id+"_img").src = map[id];
                        sign_map[id] = true;
                    }			
                };

	var pos1 = true;
	var pos2 = '0';
	var _arr = [[0, 1], [6, 7], [5], [2, 3], [12, 13]];
	function checkLi()
	{
		var isNum;
		var a = _arr[parseInt(pos2)];
		if(a.length === 1) {
			isNum = a[0];
		} else {
			isNum = pos1 ? a[1] : a[0];
		}
		pos1 = !pos1;
		rTab1.childShow(isNum, pos2);
	}
	var financeRankTab = function () {
		var li_dom  = null,
			li_len  = 0,
			c_name  = '',
			r_type  = 0,
			callback= '',
			timer;
		function G(val) { return document.getElementById(val)}
		function show (val, cb, cls) {
			li_dom = G(val).getElementsByTagName('li');
			li_len = li_dom.length;
			c_name = cls || 'current';
			callback = cb;
		}
		function child_show (val, i) {
			pos2 = i;
			// 清除记时器
			// clearTimeout(timer);
			r_type = val;
			for (var i = 0; i < li_len; i++) {
				li_dom[i].className = '';
			}
			li_dom[pos2].className = c_name;
			getResult();	
			if( val == 5 ) {
				G('zd_type').innerHTML  = '量比';
				G('zd_type').className  = 'zdfj_01';
			} else if ( val == 9 ) {
				G('zd_type').innerHTML  = '换手率';
				G('zd_type').className  = 'zdfj_01';
			} else if ( val == 2 || val == 3 || val == 12 || val == 13 ) {
 				G('zd_type').innerHTML  = "涨跌幅";
				if(val==3 || val == 13 )
				{
					G('zd_type').className  = 'zdfj_02';
				}else
				{
					G('zd_type').className  = 'zdfj';
				}
			} else {
				if ( val == 1 || val ==7) {
					G('zd_type').className  = 'zdfj_02';
				}else
				{
					G('zd_type').className  = 'zdfj';
				}
				G('zd_name').innerHTML  = '股票名称';
				G('zd_type').innerHTML  = '涨跌幅';
			}
		}
		function loadScript(url) {
			var ahead   = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName( "head" )[0] || document.documentElement;
			var ascript = document.createElement('script');
			ascript.src = url;
			ascript.type= 'text/javascript';
			ahead.appendChild(ascript);
			ascript.onload = ascript.onreadystatechange = function() {
				if( !ascript.readyState || /loaded|complete/.test( ascript.readyState ) ) {
					ahead.removeChild(ascript);
				}
			}
		}
		function getResult() {
			G('rankResult').innerHTML = '<img src="http://img.ifeng.com/tres/finance/deco/2011/1029/loading.gif" border="0px" width="150px" height="29px" style="margin-left: 10px; margin-top: 75px;" />';

			loadScript(url);

		}

				yb01.triggerType = "mouseover";
				yb01.init();

				function refreshCalendarClock(){
					var now = new Date();
					var time='';
					var hours=now.getHours();
					if(hours<10)
					{
						hours = "0"+hours;
					}
					time += hours+":";
					var minutes =now.getMinutes();
					if(minutes<10)
					{
						minutes = "0"+minutes;
					}
					time += minutes;
					document.getElementById("nowtime").innerHTML=time;
				} 
				refreshCalendarClock();
				setInterval('refreshCalendarClock()',2000); 
				</script>

            var yb01=new TabControl();
                yb01.addRange($('nTab4').getElementsByTagName('li'),['nTab4_Con1','nTab4_Con2']);

				function isLoginFun(url) {
					var isLogin = window['IS_LOGIN']();
					if (isLogin) {
						showInfo(true,url);
					} else {
						showInfo(false,url);
					}
				}
				function showInfo(flag,url){
					if(flag == false){
						window['GLOBAL_LOGIN']();
						window['REG_LOGIN_CALLBACK'](1, function(optionsORname) {
							window.location.href = url;
						});
					}else{
						window.location.href = url;
					}
				}

			  <script language="JavaScript">
function getEleByName(name) {
	  var returns = document.getElementsByName(name);
	  if(returns.length > 0) return returns;
	  returns = new Array();
	  var e = document.getElementsByTagName('td');
	  for(i = 0; i < e.length; i++) {
			if(e[i].getAttribute("name") == name) {
						  returns[returns.length] = e[i];
			}
	  }
	  return returns;
}
</script>

var Cookies = {};
Cookies.get = function(name){
	var arg = name + "=";
	var alen = arg.length;
	var clen = document.cookie.length;
	var i0 = 0;
	var j0 = 0;
	while(i0 < clen){
		j0 = i0 + alen;
		if (document.cookie.substring(i0, j0) == arg)
			return Cookies.getCookieVal(j0);
		i0 = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i0) + 1;
		if(i0 == 0)
			break;
	}
	return null;
};
Cookies.getCookieVal = function(offset){
	var endstr = document.cookie.indexOf(";", offset);
	if(endstr == -1){
		endstr = document.cookie.length;
	}
	return decodeURIComponent(document.cookie.substring(offset, endstr));
};

function search_sz(formName,search_type)
{
	var key_v;
	if(search_type=='stockDown')
	{
		key_v=document.getElementById('q1').value;
	}else if(search_type=='zijinDown')
	{
		key_v=document.getElementById('q2').value;
	}else
	{
		key_v=document.getElementById('q').value;
	}
	if(search_type == 'stock' || search_type == 'stockDown' )
	{
		sctionUrl = 'http://app.finance.ifeng.com/hq/search.php?type=stock&q='+key_v;
	}else
	{
		sctionUrl = 'http://app.finance.ifeng.com/hq/search.php?type=stock&search_type=zijin&q='+key_v;
	}
	window.open(sctionUrl);
}

<script >
//最近访问
/**
 * This js provide a simple way to operate cookie in javascript
 * function getCookie(name);
 * function setCookie(name,value[,expireDays]);
 * function deleteCookie(name);
 */
function getCookie(name)
{
    var arg = name + "=";
    var alen = arg.length;
    var clen = document.cookie.length;
    var i = 0;
    while (i < clen)
    {
        var j = i + alen;
        if (document.cookie.substring(i, j) == arg)
            return getCookieVal(j);
        i = document.cookie.indexOf(" ", i) + 1;
        if (i == 0) break;
    }
    return "";
}

function setCookie(name, value)
{
    var domain = 'finance.ifeng.com';
    var path = '/';
    
    var argv = setCookie.arguments;
    var argc = setCookie.arguments.length;
    var expDay = (argc > 2) ? argv[2] : -1;
    try
    {
        expDay = parseInt(expDay);
    }
    catch(e)
    {
        expDay = -1;
    }
    if(expDay < 0) {
        setCookieVal(name, value, null, path, domain);
    } else {
        var expDate = new Date();
        // The expDate is the date when the cookie should expire, we will keep it for a month
        expDate.setTime(expDate.getTime() + (expDay * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        
        //setCookieVal(name, value, expDate, path);
        setCookieVal(name, value, expDate, path, domain);
    }
}

function deleteCookie(name)
{
    var exp = new Date();
    exp.setTime(exp.getTime() - 1);
    // This cookie is history
    var cval = getCookie(name);
    document.cookie = name + "=" + cval + "; expires=" + exp.toGMTString();
}

function getCookieVal(offset)
{
    var endstr = document.cookie.indexOf(";", offset);
    if (endstr == -1)
        endstr = document.cookie.length;
    return unescape(document.cookie.substring(offset, endstr));
}

function setCookieVal(name, value)
{
    var argv = setCookieVal.arguments;
    var argc = setCookieVal.arguments.length;
    var expires = (argc > 2) ? argv[2] : null;
    var path = (argc > 3) ? argv[3] : null;
    var domain = (argc > 4) ? argv[4] : null;
    var secure = (argc > 5) ? argv[5] : false;
    document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) +
                      ((expires == null || expires < 0) ? "" : ("; expires=" + expires.toGMTString())) +
                      ((path == null) ? "" : ("; path=" + path)) +
                      ((domain == null) ? "" : ("; domain=" + domain)) +
                      ((secure == true) ? "; secure" : "");
}
var setUsersSaw = function(cookiename, code, expDay) {
    var user_saw_list = getCookie(cookiename);
    if (code != '') {
        if (user_saw_list == '') {
             user_saw_list += code;
        } else {
            var temp_arr = code.split(':');
            var sign = temp_arr[0]+':'+temp_arr[1]; //代码:名称
            var arr = user_saw_list.split(',');
            var dot_sign = false;
            if (arr.length < 20) {
                if (user_saw_list.indexOf(sign) != -1) {//该内容的代码和名称已经存在
					user_saw_list = '';
                    for (var i in arr) {
                        if (arr[i].indexOf(sign) != -1) {//去除
                            
                        } else {
                            user_saw_list = arr[i] + ',';
                            dot_sign = true;
                        }
                    }
                    if (dot_sign == true) {
                        user_saw_list = user_saw_list.substr(0, user_saw_list.length-1);
                    }
                }
                user_saw_list += ',' + code;
            } else {//当已经浏览过20只时，则删除最早的一只，补充新进的一只
                for (i = 1; i < 20; i++) {
                    user_saw_list += code + ',' + arr[i];
                }
                user_saw_list += code;
            }
        }
    }
    setCookie(cookiename, user_saw_list, expDay);
};
setUsersSaw('user_saw_channel_map', 'stock:股票:'+(new Date()).getTime(), 10000);

function display_hot_stock(type)
{
	var index = 0;
	for(var code in json_q)
	{
		var last = json_q[code][0];
		var chg = json_q[code][2];
		var chg_pct = json_q[code][3];
		var color = '';
		if (chg_pct > 0) {
			color = "color_red fl14";
		} else if (chg_pct < 0) {
			color = "glv fl14";
		}
		var str = '';

		str += '<td class="'+color+'">';
		str += ((last == undefined) ? '0' : YouFeng._formatNumber(last,2));
		str += '</td>';
		str += '<td class="'+color+'">';		
		str += ((chg_pct == undefined) ? '0%' : YouFeng._formatNumber(chg_pct,2)+'%');
		str += '</td>';
		str += '<td><a href="http://app.finance.ifeng.com/report/search.php?yb_search_type=stock&code='+code.substring(2)+'" target="_blank">研报</a></td>';
		jQuery("#"+type+" .tabTd:eq("+index+")").append(str);
		index++;
	}
}

function display_stock(type, str_data)
{
	if (type == "mystock3" && str_data != undefined)
	{
		var str = "";		
	}
	else
	{
		var str = '<table width="100%" border="0"><thead><tr><th width="65">股票名称</th><th width="50">股价</th><th width="65">涨跌幅</th><th>研报</th></tr></thead><tbody>';
	}
	if (str_data != undefined)
	{
		str += str_data;
	}
	else
	{
		if (typeof(json_q) == 'undefined')
		{//变量json_q没有定义
		}
		else
		{
			for(var code in json_q)
			{
				var last = json_q[code][0];
				var chg = json_q[code][2];
				var chg_pct = json_q[code][3];
				var color = '';
				var arrow_state = '';
				var yb_str = '';
				//var guba_str = '';
				if(is_usstock(code))
				{
					if (chg_pct > 0) {
						color = "glv fl14";
					} else if (chg_pct < 0) {
						color = "color_red fl14";
					}else
					{
						color = "fl14";
					}
				}
				else
				{
					if (chg_pct > 0) {
						color = "color_red fl14";
					} else if (chg_pct < 0) {
						color = "glv fl14";
					}else
					{
						color = "fl14";
					}
				}
				str += '<tr><td>';
				if (code.indexOf('hk') != -1)
				{//港股
					str += '<a href="http://finance.ifeng.com/app/hq/hkstock/'+code+'/" target="_blank">'+YouFeng.arr_data[code].substr(0,5)+'</a></td>';
					yb_str = "<td>--</td>";
				}else if(code =='sh000001' || code == 'sz399001'){
                    str += '<a href="http://finance.ifeng.com/app/hq/stock/'+code+'/" target="_blank">'+YouFeng.arr_data[code].substr(0,5)+'</a></td>';
					yb_str = "<td>--</td>";
				}else if(is_usstock(code))
				{
					str += '<a href="http://finance.ifeng.com/app/hq/usstock/'+code+'/" target="_blank">'+YouFeng.arr_data[code].substr(0,5)+'</a></td>';
					yb_str = "<td>--</td>";
				}
				else
				{
					str += '<a href="http://finance.ifeng.com/app/hq/stock/'+code+'/" target="_blank">'+YouFeng.arr_data[code].substr(0,5)+'</a></td>';
					yb_str = '<td><a href="http://app.finance.ifeng.com/report/search.php?yb_search_type=stock&code='+code.substring(2)+'" target="_blank">研报</a></td>';
				}
				str += '<td class="'+color+'">';
				str += ((last == undefined) ? '0' : YouFeng._formatNumber(last,2));
				str += '</td>';
				str += '<td class="'+color+'">';
				str += ((chg_pct == undefined) ? '0%' : YouFeng._formatNumber(chg_pct,2)+'%');
				str += '</td>';
				str += yb_str;
				str += '</tr>'; 
			}
		}
	}
	if (type == "mystock3" && str_data != undefined)
	{
	}
	else if (type == "mystock3")
	{
		str += '<tr><td colspan=5 style="text-align:right;padding-right:15px;"><a href="http://app.finance.ifeng.com/custom/mystock.php" target="_blank">查看我的自选股>></a></td></tr>';
		str += '</tbody></table>';
	}
	else
	{
		str += '</tbody></table>';
	}
	jQuery("#"+type).html(str);
}

function is_usstock(code)
{
	var pattern = "^[A-Z\.a-z]+$";
	if (code.match(pattern))
	{
		return true;
	}
	else
	{
		return false;
	}
}

function mystock3_key_evt(_evt)
{
	switch (_evt.keyCode)
	{
		case 13: //enter
			mystock3_login();
			break;
		default:
			break;
	}
}

function mystock3_login_cb(rlt_arr)
{
	eval("var _rlt_arr = "+rlt_arr+";");	// 获取json数据
	if(_rlt_arr[0] == 0)
	{
		alert("用户名或密码错误");
	}
	else 
	{
		sid = getCookie('sid');
		login_state = true;
		getMyStock();
	}
}

function mystock3_login()
{
	var username = document.getElementById("username3").value;
	var password = document.getElementById("password3").value;
	if(login_state)
	{
		var l_theurl = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/custom/logincheck.php?rn=@cache@";
		var loadjs = new LoadScript_youfeng("loadscript1", l_theurl, mystock3_login_cb, "login_rlt", "@cache@");
		loadjs.loading();
	}
	else
	{
		if(""==username||""==password)
		{
			alert("请输入用户名和密码！");
			return ;
		}
		else
		{
			var l_theurl = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/custom/logincheck.php?rn=@cache@&username="+username+"&password="+md5(password);
			var loadjs = new LoadScript_youfeng("logindatascript001", l_theurl, mystock3_login_cb, "login_rlt", "@cache@");
			loadjs.loading();
		}
	}
	return ;
}

function setUsrLogin()
{//设置登陆框
	var str = '';
	str += '<div class="login"  style="padding-top:35px;">';
	str += '	<form name="usr_login_box" action="" method="get">';
	str += '		<label><span>用户名：</span><input type="text" id="username3" name="username3" class="input_style01"></label>';
	str += '		<label><span>密&nbsp;&nbsp;码：</span><input type="password" id="password3" name="password3"  onkeydown="mystock3_key_evt(event)" class="input_style01"></label>';
	str += '        <label class="clearfix"><div class="seach_right clearfix"><a style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="javasript:mystock3_login();" class="dl">登录</a><a class="dl2" href="http://ucenter.ifeng.com/new-account" target="_blank" >注册</a></label>';
	str += '    </form>';
	str += '</div>';
	jQuery('#mystock3').removeClass('abo_02');
	display_stock('mystock3', str);
}

function getMyStock()
{
	jQuery.getJSON(
		"http://app.finance.ifeng.com/custom/api/youfeng2.php?callback=?",
		{
			sid: decodeURIComponent(escape(sid)),
			iter_type: 'mystock',	//mystock, myfund  abo_02
			req_type: 'json',
			req_num: 4
		},
		function(data){
			jQuery('#mystock3').addClass('abo_02');
			if (data != null)
			{
				var arr = Array();
				var code_str = '';
				for (key in data)
				{
					var code = data[key]["code"];
					YouFeng.arr_data[code] = data[key]["name"];
					code_str = code_str + code + ",";
				}
				code_str = code_str.substr(0, code_str.length - 1);
				jQuery.getScript('http://hq.finance.ifeng.com/q.php?l='+code_str+'&f=json&e=display_stock("mystock3");');
			}
			else
			{
				str = '<table class="tb0"><tbody id="tbodyPort"><tr><td style="line-height: 40px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153);" colspan="3">您尚未添加自选股</td></tr><tr><td style="text-align: center;" colspan="3"><span class="add_stock"><a href="http://app.finance.ifeng.com/custom/mystock.php" target="_blank">添加股票+</a></span></td></tr></tbody></table>';
				jQuery('#mystock3').removeClass('abo_02');
				display_stock('mystock3', str);				
			}
		}
	);
}

var user_saw_list = '';
eval("var user_saw_map = YouFengCookie.getCookie('user_saw_stock_map');");   //最近列表(user_saw_stock_map,user_saw_fund_map)
if (user_saw_map != '') {
	var n = 0;
	var arr = user_saw_map.split(',');
	for (var i in arr) {
		if (arr[i] != '' && n < 7)
		{
			var t = arr[i].split(':');
			YouFeng.arr_data[t[0]] = t[1];  //获取代码和名称的全局对照数组
			user_saw_list += t[0] + ',';
			n++;
		}
	}
	user_saw_list = user_saw_list.substr(0, user_saw_list.length-1);
}
if (user_saw_list != null && user_saw_list != '')
{
	jQuery.getScript("http://hq.finance.ifeng.com/q.php?l="+user_saw_list+"&f=json&e=display_stock('latest_stock');");
}
else
{
	jQuery.getScript("http://app.finance.ifeng.com/hq/hot_stock.php?type=latest_stock&num=4&style=stock");
}

if (getCookie('sid') != '') {
	sid = getCookie('sid');
	login_state = true;
    getMyStock();
}
else
{
	setUsrLogin();
}

var myDate = new Date();
var nowYear = ( myDate.getYear() < 1900 ) ? ( 1900 + myDate.getYear() ) : myDate.getYear();
var nowMonth = myDate.getMonth()+1;
var nowDay = myDate.getDate();
if(nowMonth < 10){
	nowMonth = "0"+nowMonth;
}
if(nowDay < 10){
	nowDay = "0"+nowDay;
}
nowDate = nowYear+nowMonth+nowDay;
var vote_dkdc_result_url = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/vote/vote_result.php?type=dkdc"+nowDate;
var vote_cwdc_result_url = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/vote/vote_result.php?type=cwdc"+nowDate;
getScript_cds(vote_dkdc_result_url, init_votes);
setTimeout("getScript_cds(vote_cwdc_result_url, init_votes)", 1000);

function vote(type, id)
{
 jQuery.getScript("http://app.finance.ifeng.com/vote/vote.php?type="+type+nowDate+"&id="+id+"&callback=add_one");
}
function add_one(id)
{
 var old = parseInt(jQuery("#vote_result_"+id).html());
 if (isNaN(old) == true)
 {
  jQuery("#vote_result_"+id).html(1);
 }
 else
 {
  jQuery("#vote_result_"+id).html(old+1);
 }
}
function init_votes()
{
	var all_vote_num = vote_result["all"];
	for(var id in vote_result)
	{
	 var vote_pct = 0;
	 if (all_vote_num)
	 {
		vote_pct = (vote_result[id]/all_vote_num*100).toFixed(1)+"%";
	 }
	 jQuery("#vote_result_"+id).html(vote_result[id]);
	 jQuery("#vote_result_pic_"+id).animate({width:vote_pct}, "slow");
	}
}

<script>
function yb_search_stock(form)
{
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].action = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/hq/search.php";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].type.disabled = false;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].select_type.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].select_code.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].keyword.disabled = false;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].authortxt.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].titletxt.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].ind_code.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].org_code.disabled = true;

	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].keyword.style.display = "inline";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].org_code.style.display = "none";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].authortxt.style.display = "none";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].titletxt.style.display = "none";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].ind_code.style.display = "none";
}

function yb_search_org(form)
{
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].action = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/report/search.php";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].type.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].select_type.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].select_code.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].keyword.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].authortxt.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].titletxt.disabled = true;
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].ind_code.disabled = true;

	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].org_code.disabled = false;

	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].org_code.style.display = "inline";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].authortxt.style.display = "none";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].titletxt.style.display = "none";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].ind_code.style.display = "none";
	document.getElementsByName(form)[0].keyword.style.display = "none";
}

var Suggest_hq =
{
	line : 0,
	count : 0,
	keyword : "",
	type : "all",
	form : "",
	list_id : "",
	suggesttype : "",
	move : function (_evt)
	{
		switch (_evt.keyCode)
		{
			case 38: //up
				if (this.line > 1)
				{
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "";
					this.line = this.line - 1;
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "current";
				}
				break;
			case 40: //down
				if (this.line > 0 && this.line < this.count)
				{
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "";
				}
				if (this.line < this.count)
				{
					this.line = this.line + 1;
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "current";
				}
				break;
			case 13: //enter
				if (this.line >= 1 && this.line <= this.count)
				{
					document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_type.disabled = false;
					document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_code.disabled = false;
					document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_type.value = suggest_json[this.line-1]["t"];
					document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_code.value = suggest_json[this.line-1]["c"];
					if (this.suggesttype == "yjyg")
					{
						window.open('http://app.finance.ifeng.com/data/stock/yjyg.php?symbol='+suggest_json[this.line-1]["s"]);
					}					
				}
				break;
			default:
				
				break;
		}

	},
	display : function (_display)
	{
		if (_display == "inline")
		{				
			var table_html = document.getElementById(this.list_id).innerHTML;
			if (table_html != "")
			{
				document.getElementById(this.list_id).style.display = _display;
			}
		}
		else if (_display == "none")
		{
			document.getElementById(this.list_id).style.display = _display;
		}
	},
	mark_keyword : function (_str, _keyword)
	{
		return _str.replace(_keyword, "<span>"+_keyword+"</span>");
	},
	work : function ()
	{
		var _type_conf = {"stock":"股票","fund":"基金","hkstock":"港股","forex":"外汇","bond":"债券"};

		var table_html = "";

		this.line = 0;
		this.count = 0;

		document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_type.disabled = true;
		document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_code.disabled = true;
		document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_type.value = "";
		document.getElementsByName(this.form)[0].select_code.value = "";
		
		for(var i=0; i<suggest_json.length; i++)
		{
			this.count++;

			var code = suggest_json[i]["c"];
			var symbol = suggest_json[i]["s"];
			var name = suggest_json[i]["n"];
			var pinyin = suggest_json[i]["p"];
			var type = suggest_json[i]["t"];
			
			var _type = _type_conf[type];

			var bgcolor = "";
			if (i % 2 == 1)
			{
				bgcolor = "bgcolor='#F5F5F5'";
			}

			if (type == "forex")
			{
				table_html += "  <tr id=\"suggest_"+(parseInt(i)+1)+"\" onmouseover=\"javascript:this.className='current';this.style.cursor='pointer'\" onmouseout=\"javascript:this.className=''\" onclick=\"javascript:window.open('http://finance.ifeng.com/app/hq/"+type+"/"+symbol+"/')\" >";
			}
			else 
			{
				var code_begin = code.substring(0,4);
				var open_url = "http://finance.ifeng.com/app/hq/"+type+"/"+code+"/";
				if (this.suggesttype == "yjyg")
				{
					open_url = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/data/stock/yjyg.php?symbol="+symbol;
				}
				if (this.type == "report" && (code_begin == "sh60" || code_begin == "sz00" || code_begin == "sz30"))
				{
					open_url = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/report/search.php?yb_search_type=stock&code="+code.substr(2);
				}
				table_html += "  <tr id=\"suggest_"+(parseInt(i)+1)+"\" onmouseover=\"javascript:this.className='current';this.style.cursor='pointer'\" onmouseout=\"javascript:this.className=''\" onclick=\"javascript:window.open('"+open_url+"')\" >";
			}
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+Suggest_hq.mark_keyword(symbol.toUpperCase(), this.keyword.toUpperCase())+"</td>";
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+Suggest_hq.mark_keyword(name, this.keyword)+"</td>";
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+Suggest_hq.mark_keyword(pinyin.toUpperCase(), this.keyword.toUpperCase())+"</td>";
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+_type+"</td>";
			table_html += "  </tr>";

		}
		if (table_html != "")
		{
			table_html = "<table width='100%' border='0' cellspacing='0' cellpadding='0' class='tab'>"+table_html+"</table>";
		}
		document.getElementById(this.list_id).innerHTML = table_html;
		if (table_html != "")
		{				
			Suggest_hq.display("inline");
		}
		else
		{
			Suggest_hq.display("none");
		}
	},
	typewrite : function (_keyword)
	{
		if (_keyword != this.keyword)
		{
			this.keyword = _keyword;
			var oHead = document.getElementsByTagName('HEAD').item(0);
			var oScript = document.createElement("script");
			oScript.type = "text/javascript";
			oScript.src = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/hq/suggest_v2.php?t="+this.type+"&q="+_keyword+"&cb=Suggest_hq.work();";
			oHead.appendChild(oScript); 
		}
		
	}
}

var Suggest_v3 =
{
	line : 0,
	count : 0,
	keyword : "",
	move : function (_evt)
	{
		switch (_evt.keyCode)
		{
			case 38: //up
				if (this.line > 1)
				{
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "";
					this.line = this.line - 1;
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "current";
				}
				break;
			case 40: //down
				if (this.line > 0 && this.line < this.count)
				{
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "";
				}
				if (this.line < this.count)
				{
					this.line = this.line + 1;
					document.getElementById("suggest_"+this.line).className = "current";
				}
				break;
			case 13: //enter
				if (this.line >= 1 && this.line <= this.count)
				{
					window.open('http://lhb.finance.ifeng.com/detail.php?code='+suggest_json[this.line-1]["s"]);
				}
				break;
			default:
				
				break;
		}

	},
	display : function (_display)
	{
		if (_display == "inline")
		{
			var table_html = document.getElementById("suggest_list_longhubang").innerHTML;
			if (table_html != "")
			{
				document.getElementById("suggest_list_longhubang").style.display = _display;
			}
		}
		else if (_display == "none")
		{
			document.getElementById("suggest_list_longhubang").style.display = _display;
		}
	},
	mark_keyword : function (_str, _keyword)
	{
		return _str.replace(_keyword, "<span>"+_keyword+"</span>");
	},
	work : function ()
	{
		var _type_conf = {"stock":"股票","fund":"基金","hkstock":"港股","forex":"外汇","bond":"债券"};

		var table_html = "";

		this.line = 0;
		this.count = 0;
		
		for(var i=0; i<suggest_json.length; i++)
		{
			if (suggest_json[i]["t"] != "stock")
			{
				continue;
			}
			
			if (suggest_json[i]["c"].substr(0,4) != "sh60" && suggest_json[i]["c"].substr(0,4) != "sz00")
			{//过滤掉指数
				continue;
			}

			this.count++;

			var code = suggest_json[i]["c"];
			var symbol = suggest_json[i]["s"];
			var name = suggest_json[i]["n"];
			var pinyin = suggest_json[i]["p"];
			var type = suggest_json[i]["t"];
			
			var _type = _type_conf[type];

			var bgcolor = "";
			if (i % 2 == 1)
			{
				bgcolor = "bgcolor='#F5F5F5'";
			}
			
			if (i == 0) {
				document.getElementById("code_like").value = symbol;	//将近似的code输入到form表单中
			}
			
			table_html += "  <tr id=\"suggest_"+(parseInt(i)+1)+"\" onclick=\"window.open('http://lhb.finance.ifeng.com/detail.php?code="+symbol+"');\" onmouseover=\"javascript:this.className='current';this.style.cursor='pointer'\" onmouseout=\"javascript:this.className=''\">";
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+Suggest_v3.mark_keyword(symbol.toUpperCase(), this.keyword.toUpperCase())+"</td>";
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+Suggest_v3.mark_keyword(name, this.keyword)+"</td>";
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+Suggest_v3.mark_keyword(pinyin.toUpperCase(), this.keyword.toUpperCase())+"</td>";
			table_html += "    <td "+bgcolor+">"+_type+"</td>";
			table_html += "  </tr>";
		}
		if (table_html != "")
		{
			table_html = "<table width='100%' border='0' cellspacing='0' cellpadding='0' class='tab'>"+table_html+"</table>";
		}
		document.getElementById("suggest_list_longhubang").innerHTML = table_html;
		if (table_html != "")
		{
			Suggest_v3.display("inline");
		}
		else
		{
			Suggest_v3.display("none");
		}
	},
	typewrite : function (_keyword)
	{
		if (_keyword != this.keyword)
		{
			this.keyword = _keyword;
			
			var oHead = document.getElementsByTagName('HEAD').item(0);
			var oScript = document.createElement("script");
			oScript.type = "text/javascript";
			oScript.src = "http://app.finance.ifeng.com/hq/suggest_v2.php?t=stock&q="+_keyword+"&cb=Suggest_v3.work();";
			oHead.appendChild(oScript); 
		}
		
	}
}
var longhubang_form_submit = function() {
	var code = jQuery("#code_like").val();
	var url = "http://lhb.finance.ifeng.com/detail.php?code="+code;
	window.open(url);
	return false;
}
</script>
<script>
var dh;
var dw;
var left;
var top;
var gotobtnH=600;
var closeweixin=false;

jQuery(window).resize(function() {
	jQuery("#addweixin").css("right",jQuery(document).width()/2-600);
	jQuery("#addweixin").css("top",jQuery(window).height()+jQuery(window).scrollTop()-180);
	jQuery("#addweixin1").css("right",jQuery(document).width()/2-600);
});
jQuery("#addweixin").css("position","absolute");
jQuery("#addweixin").css("top",jQuery(window).height()+jQuery(window).scrollTop()-180);
jQuery("#addweixin").css("right",jQuery(document).width()/2-600);
jQuery("#addweixin1").css("right",jQuery(document).width()/2-600);
var awstoptime;
var awctop={st:0,et:0};
var wscrolltop=0;
jQuery(window).scroll(function () {
	dw = jQuery(document).width();
	left = (dw / 2 + 512);
	jQuery("#gotopbtn").css("bottom", "5px");
	jQuery("#gotopbtn").css("left", left + "px");
	
	if (jQuery(window).scrollTop() > 600) {
		jQuery("#gotopbtn").css("bottom", "5px");
		jQuery("#gotopbtn").fadeIn("slow");
	}
	else {
		jQuery("#gotopbtn").fadeOut("slow");				
	}
	
	awctop.st=parseFloat(jQuery("#addweixin").offset().top);
	awctop.et=jQuery(window).scrollTop()+jQuery(window).height()-180;
	
	clearInterval(awstoptime);
	if(closeweixin==false){
	
	if(wscrolltop>jQuery(window).scrollTop()){
		jQuery("#addweixin").hide();
		jQuery("#addweixin1").show();
		jQuery("#addweixin1").css("bottom",20);
		jQuery("#addweixin").css("top",jQuery(window).scrollTop()+jQuery(window).height()-180);
	}
	else{
		jQuery("#addweixin1").hide();
		jQuery("#addweixin").show();
		jQuery("#addweixin").css("position","absolute");
		var tmpnum=0;
		awstoptime=setInterval(function(){
	jQuery("#addweixin").stop();
			var awxmtop=0;
			if(awctop.st<awctop.et){
				awxmtop=parseFloat(jQuery("#addweixin").css("top"))+((awctop.et-awctop.st)/10);
				if(awxmtop>awctop.et){
					awxmtop=awctop.et;
					jQuery("#addweixin").css("top",awxmtop);
					clearInterval(awstoptime);
					jQuery("#addweixin").animate({top:awxmtop+30},300).animate({top:awxmtop-20},300).animate({top:awxmtop},300);
				}
			}
			else{
				jQuery("#addweixin").hide();
				jQuery("#addweixin1").show();
				awxmtop=jQuery(window).scrollTop()+jQuery(window).height()-180;
			}
			
			jQuery("#addweixin").css("top",awxmtop);
			
		},30);
	}
	wscrolltop=jQuery(window).scrollTop();
	}
});
jQuery(".close_btn").click(function(){
	jQuery(this).parent().hide();
	closeweixin=true;
});
</script>
